generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client"
  output   = "../src/generated/prisma"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "mysql"
}

enum RecordStatus {
  ACTIVE
  INACTIVE
  ARCHIVED
}

enum EmployeeStatus {
  ACTIVE
  INACTIVE
  RESIGNED
  TERMINATED
  ON_LEAVE
}

enum UserStatus {
  ACTIVE
  INACTIVE
  DISABLED
}

enum RfidStatus {
  ACTIVE
  DISABLED
  LOST
  REPLACED
}

enum AttendanceStatus {
  ON_TIME
  LATE
  HALF_DAY
  ABSENT
  EXCUSED
  PENDING_REVIEW
  MISSING_TIMEOUT
}

enum AttendanceSource {
  RFID
  WEB
  MANUAL
  KIOSK
  MOBILE
}

enum PunchType {
  TIME_IN
  TIME_OUT
  REPEATED_SCAN
  MANUAL_EDIT
  CORRECTION
}

enum LeaveStatus {
  PENDING
  APPROVED
  REJECTED
  CANCELLED
}

enum NoticeStatus {
  DRAFT
  PUBLISHED
  ARCHIVED
}

enum NoticeAudience {
  ALL
  HR_ADMIN
  HEADS
  STAFF_FACULTY_MAINTENANCE
}

enum EducationLevel {
  ELEMENTARY
  SECONDARY
  VOCATIONAL
  COLLEGE
  MASTERS
  DOCTORATE
}

enum AttendanceExceptionType {
  HOLIDAY
  CLASS_SUSPENSION
  NO_WORK
  SCHOOL_EVENT
  REST_DAY
  OTHER
}

model Branch {
  branchId   Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("branch_id")
  branchCode String       @unique @map("branch_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name       String       @db.VarChar(191)
  address    String?      @db.Text
  latitude   Decimal?     @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  longitude  Decimal?     @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  radiusM    Int?         @map("radius_m")
  status     RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt  DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt  DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employees            Employee[]
  notices              Notice[]
  attendanceInRecords  Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceInBranch")
  attendanceOutRecords Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceOutBranch")
  attendanceLogs       AttendanceLog[]

  @@map("branches")
}

model Department {
  departmentId   Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("department_id")
  departmentCode String       @unique @map("department_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name           String       @db.VarChar(191)
  status         RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt      DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt      DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employees Employee[]
  notices   Notice[]

  @@map("departments")
}

model Designation {
  designationId   Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("designation_id")
  designationCode String       @unique @map("designation_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name            String       @db.VarChar(191)
  status          RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt       DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt       DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employees Employee[]

  @@map("designations")
}

model EmpType {
  empTypeId   Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("emp_type_id")
  empTypeCode String       @unique @map("emp_type_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name        String       @db.VarChar(191)
  status      RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt   DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employees Employee[]

  @@map("emp_types")
}

model Employee {
  empId         Int            @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("emp_id")
  empNumber     String         @unique @map("emp_number") @db.VarChar(80)
  prc           String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  lastName      String         @map("last_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  firstName     String         @map("first_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  middleName    String?        @map("middle_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  gender        String?        @db.VarChar(30)
  dob           DateTime?      @db.Date
  pob           String?        @db.VarChar(191)
  email         String?        @unique @db.VarChar(191)
  phone         String?        @db.VarChar(40)
  landline      String?        @db.VarChar(40)
  civilStatus   String?        @map("civil_status") @db.VarChar(60)
  citizenship   String?        @db.VarChar(100)
  address       String?        @db.Text
  branchId      Int            @map("branch_id")
  departmentId  Int?           @map("department_id")
  designationId Int?           @map("designation_id")
  empTypeId     Int?           @map("emp_type_id")
  scheduleId    Int?           @map("schedule_id")
  isFlexible    Boolean        @default(false) @map("is_flexible")
  avLeave       Float          @default(0) @map("av_leave")
  sss           String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  pagibig       String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  philhealth    String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  tin           String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  img           String?        @db.VarChar(255)
  dateHired     DateTime?      @map("date_hired") @db.Date
  dateSigned    DateTime?      @map("date_signed") @db.Date
  status        EmployeeStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt     DateTime       @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt     DateTime       @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  branch      Branch         @relation(fields: [branchId], references: [branchId], onDelete: Restrict)
  department  Department?    @relation(fields: [departmentId], references: [departmentId], onDelete: SetNull)
  designation Designation?   @relation(fields: [designationId], references: [designationId], onDelete: SetNull)
  empType     EmpType?       @relation(fields: [empTypeId], references: [empTypeId], onDelete: SetNull)
  schedule    ShiftSchedule? @relation("EmployeeCurrentSchedule", fields: [scheduleId], references: [scheduleId], onDelete: SetNull)

  user                        User?
  rfidCards                   RfidCard[]
  attendanceRecords           Attendance[]
  attendanceLogs              AttendanceLog[]
  leaves                      Leave[]
  employeeScheduleAssignments EmployeeScheduleAssignment[]
  familyBackground            EmployeeFamilyBackground?
  children                    EmployeeChild[]
  educationSummary            EmployeeEducationSummary?
  educationalBackgrounds      EmployeeEducationalBackground[]
  workExperiences             EmployeeWorkExperience[]
  contract                    EmployeeContract?

  @@index([branchId])
  @@index([departmentId])
  @@index([designationId])
  @@index([empTypeId])
  @@index([scheduleId])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("employees")
}

model EmployeeFamilyBackground {
  familyBackgroundId Int      @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("family_background_id")
  empId              Int      @unique @map("emp_id")

  fatherLastName     String?  @map("father_last_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  fatherFirstName    String?  @map("father_first_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  fatherMiddleName   String?  @map("father_middle_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  fatherAddress      String?  @map("father_address") @db.Text
  fatherOccupation   String?  @map("father_occupation") @db.VarChar(191)

  motherLastName     String?  @map("mother_last_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  motherFirstName    String?  @map("mother_first_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  motherMiddleName   String?  @map("mother_middle_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  motherAddress      String?  @map("mother_address") @db.Text
  motherOccupation   String?  @map("mother_occupation") @db.VarChar(191)

  spouseLastName     String?  @map("spouse_last_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  spouseFirstName    String?  @map("spouse_first_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  spouseMiddleName   String?  @map("spouse_middle_name") @db.VarChar(100)
  spouseAddress      String?  @map("spouse_address") @db.Text
  spouseOccupation   String?  @map("spouse_occupation") @db.VarChar(191)

  employer           String?  @db.VarChar(191)
  employerAddress    String?  @map("employer_address") @db.Text
  employerPhone      String?  @map("employer_phone") @db.VarChar(40)

  createdAt          DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt          DateTime @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee           Employee @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@map("employee_family_backgrounds")
}

model EmployeeChild {
  childId     Int       @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("child_id")
  empId       Int       @map("emp_id")
  fullName    String    @map("full_name") @db.VarChar(191)
  dateOfBirth DateTime? @map("date_of_birth") @db.Date
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt   DateTime  @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee    Employee  @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@index([empId])
  @@map("employee_children")
}

model EmployeeEducationSummary {
  educationSummaryId Int      @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("education_summary_id")
  empId              Int      @unique @map("emp_id")
  letPasser          Boolean  @default(false) @map("let_passer")
  createdAt          DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt          DateTime @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee           Employee @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@map("employee_education_summaries")
}

model EmployeeEducationalBackground {
  educationalBackgroundId Int            @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("educational_background_id")
  empId                   Int            @map("emp_id")
  level                   EducationLevel
  schoolName              String?        @map("school_name") @db.VarChar(191)
  yearGraduated           String?        @map("year_graduated") @db.VarChar(50)
  course                  String?        @db.VarChar(191)
  units                   String?        @db.VarChar(80)
  academicHonors          String?        @map("academic_honors") @db.VarChar(191)
  address                 String?        @db.Text
  createdAt               DateTime       @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt               DateTime       @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee                Employee       @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@unique([empId, level])
  @@index([empId])
  @@map("employee_educational_backgrounds")
}

model EmployeeWorkExperience {
  workExperienceId Int      @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("work_experience_id")
  empId            Int      @map("emp_id")
  company          String   @db.VarChar(191)
  position         String   @db.VarChar(191)
  inclusiveDates   String?  @map("inclusive_dates") @db.VarChar(191)
  createdAt        DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt        DateTime @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee         Employee @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@index([empId])
  @@map("employee_work_experiences")
}

model EmployeeContract {
  contractId    Int      @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("contract_id")
  empId         Int      @unique @map("emp_id")
  dateHired     DateTime @map("date_hired") @db.Date
  dateOfJoining DateTime @map("date_of_joining") @db.Date
  signature     String   @db.VarChar(255)
  dateSigned    DateTime @map("date_signed") @db.Date
  createdAt     DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt     DateTime @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee      Employee @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@map("employee_contracts")
}

model Role {
  roleId      Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("role_id")
  code        String       @unique @db.VarChar(80)
  name        String       @db.VarChar(120)
  description String?      @db.Text
  status      RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt   DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  users           User[]
  rolePermissions RolePermission[]

  @@map("roles")
}

model Permission {
  permissionId Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("permission_id")
  code         String       @unique @db.VarChar(120)
  name         String       @db.VarChar(150)
  module       String       @db.VarChar(80)
  description  String?      @db.Text
  status       RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt    DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt    DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  rolePermissions RolePermission[]

  @@index([module])
  @@map("permissions")
}

model RolePermission {
  roleId       Int      @map("role_id")
  permissionId Int      @map("permission_id")
  createdAt    DateTime @default(now()) @map("created_at")

  role       Role       @relation(fields: [roleId], references: [roleId], onDelete: Cascade)
  permission Permission @relation(fields: [permissionId], references: [permissionId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@id([roleId, permissionId])
  @@index([permissionId])
  @@map("role_permissions")
}

model User {
  userId             Int        @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("user_id")
  empId              Int?       @unique @map("emp_id")
  username           String     @unique @db.VarChar(191)
  email              String     @unique @db.VarChar(191)
  passwordHash       String     @map("password_hash") @db.VarChar(255)
  roleId             Int        @map("role_id")
  mustChangePassword Boolean    @default(true) @map("must_change_password")
  failedAttempts     Int        @default(0) @map("failed_attempts")
  isLocked           Boolean    @default(false) @map("is_locked")
  lockoutUntil       DateTime?  @map("lockout_until")
  lastLoginAt        DateTime?  @map("last_login_at")
  status             UserStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt          DateTime   @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt          DateTime   @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee Employee? @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: SetNull)
  role     Role      @relation(fields: [roleId], references: [roleId], onDelete: Restrict)

  verifiedAttendances Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceVerifiedBy")
  approvedAttendances Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceApprovedBy")
  createdAttendances  Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceCreatedBy")
  updatedAttendances  Attendance[] @relation("AttendanceUpdatedBy")
  assignedSchedules   EmployeeScheduleAssignment[] @relation("ScheduleAssignedBy")
  approvedLeaves      Leave[] @relation("LeaveApprovedBy")
  createdLeaves       Leave[] @relation("LeaveCreatedBy")
  notices             Notice[] @relation("NoticeCreatedBy")
  noticeReads         NoticeRead[]
  updatedNotices      Notice[] @relation("NoticeUpdatedBy")
  activityLogs        ActivityLog[]

  @@index([roleId])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("users")
}

model Shift {
  shiftId      Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("shift_id")
  shiftCode    String       @unique @map("shift_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name         String       @db.VarChar(120)
  startTime    String       @map("start_time") @db.VarChar(8)
  endTime      String       @map("end_time") @db.VarChar(8)
  graceMinutes Int          @default(0) @map("grace_minutes")
  isOvernight  Boolean      @default(false) @map("is_overnight")
  status       RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt    DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt    DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  schedules ShiftSchedule[]

  @@map("shifts")
}

model ShiftSchedule {
  scheduleId    Int          @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("schedule_id")
  shiftId       Int          @map("shift_id")
  scheduleCode  String       @unique @map("schedule_code") @db.VarChar(50)
  name          String       @db.VarChar(120)
  daysOfWeek    String?      @map("days_of_week") @db.VarChar(50)
  effectiveFrom DateTime     @map("effective_from") @db.Date
  effectiveTo   DateTime?    @map("effective_to") @db.Date
  status        RecordStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt     DateTime     @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt     DateTime     @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  shift                    Shift                        @relation(fields: [shiftId], references: [shiftId], onDelete: Restrict)
  currentEmployees         Employee[]                   @relation("EmployeeCurrentSchedule")
  employeeAssignments      EmployeeScheduleAssignment[]
  attendanceRecords        Attendance[]

  @@index([shiftId])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("shift_schedules")
}

model EmployeeScheduleAssignment {
  assignmentId Int       @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("assignment_id")
  empId        Int       @map("emp_id")
  scheduleId   Int       @map("schedule_id")
  validFrom    DateTime  @map("valid_from") @db.Date
  validTo      DateTime? @map("valid_to") @db.Date
  isActive     Boolean   @default(true) @map("is_active")
  assignedById Int?      @map("assigned_by")
  remarks      String?   @db.Text
  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt    DateTime  @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee   Employee      @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)
  schedule   ShiftSchedule @relation(fields: [scheduleId], references: [scheduleId], onDelete: Restrict)
  assignedBy User?         @relation("ScheduleAssignedBy", fields: [assignedById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)

  @@index([empId])
  @@index([scheduleId])
  @@index([assignedById])
  @@index([isActive])
  @@map("employee_schedule_assignments")
}

model RfidCard {
  rfidId     Int        @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("rfid_id")
  empId      Int        @map("emp_id")
  rfidUid    String     @map("rfid_uid") @db.VarChar(191)
  status     RfidStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  assignedAt DateTime   @default(now()) @map("assigned_at")
  disabledAt DateTime?  @map("disabled_at")
  remarks    String?    @db.Text
  createdAt  DateTime   @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt  DateTime   @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee Employee @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@unique([rfidUid, status])
  @@index([empId])
  @@index([rfidUid])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("rfid_cards")
}

model Attendance {
  attendanceId Int       @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("attendance_id")
  empId        Int       @map("emp_id")
  scheduleId   Int?      @map("schedule_id")
  attDate      DateTime  @map("att_date") @db.Date

  timeIn      DateTime?        @map("time_in")
  inRemark    String?          @map("in_remark") @db.VarChar(120)
  inReason    String?          @map("in_reason") @db.Text
  inLatitude  Decimal?         @map("in_latitude") @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  inLongitude Decimal?         @map("in_longitude") @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  inPhoto     String?          @map("in_photo") @db.VarChar(255)
  inSource    AttendanceSource? @map("in_source")
  inBranchId  Int?             @map("in_branch_id")
  inAddress   String?          @map("in_address") @db.Text

  timeOut      DateTime?        @map("time_out")
  outRemark    String?          @map("out_remark") @db.VarChar(120)
  outReason    String?          @map("out_reason") @db.Text
  outLatitude  Decimal?         @map("out_latitude") @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  outLongitude Decimal?         @map("out_longitude") @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  outPhoto     String?          @map("out_photo") @db.VarChar(255)
  outSource    AttendanceSource? @map("out_source")
  outBranchId  Int?             @map("out_branch_id")
  outAddress   String?          @map("out_address") @db.Text

  status       AttendanceStatus @default(PENDING_REVIEW)
  totalMinutes Int?             @map("total_minutes")
  isSynced     Boolean          @default(true) @map("is_synced")
  isManual     Boolean          @default(false) @map("is_manual")

  verifiedById Int?      @map("verified_by")
  verifiedAt   DateTime? @map("verified_at")
  approvedById Int?      @map("approved_by")
  approvedAt   DateTime? @map("approved_at")
  createdById  Int?      @map("created_by")
  updatedById  Int?      @map("updated_by")
  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt    DateTime  @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee   Employee       @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)
  schedule   ShiftSchedule? @relation(fields: [scheduleId], references: [scheduleId], onDelete: SetNull)
  inBranch   Branch?        @relation("AttendanceInBranch", fields: [inBranchId], references: [branchId], onDelete: SetNull)
  outBranch  Branch?        @relation("AttendanceOutBranch", fields: [outBranchId], references: [branchId], onDelete: SetNull)
  verifiedBy User?          @relation("AttendanceVerifiedBy", fields: [verifiedById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)
  approvedBy User?          @relation("AttendanceApprovedBy", fields: [approvedById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)
  createdBy  User?          @relation("AttendanceCreatedBy", fields: [createdById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)
  updatedBy  User?          @relation("AttendanceUpdatedBy", fields: [updatedById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)
  logs       AttendanceLog[]

  @@unique([empId, attDate])
  @@index([scheduleId])
  @@index([attDate])
  @@index([status])
  @@index([inBranchId])
  @@index([outBranchId])
  @@index([verifiedById])
  @@index([approvedById])
  @@index([createdById])
  @@index([updatedById])
  @@map("attendance")
}

model AttendanceLog {
  logId        Int              @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("log_id")
  attendanceId Int             @map("attendance_id")
  empId        Int             @map("emp_id")
  punchType    PunchType       @map("punch_type")
  punchedAt    DateTime        @default(now()) @map("punched_at")
  latitude     Decimal?        @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  longitude    Decimal?        @db.Decimal(10, 7)
  photo        String?         @db.VarChar(255)
  address      String?         @db.Text
  source       AttendanceSource
  branchId     Int?            @map("branch_id")
  remarks      String?         @db.VarChar(120)
  reason       String?         @db.Text
  createdAt    DateTime        @default(now()) @map("created_at")

  attendance Attendance @relation(fields: [attendanceId], references: [attendanceId], onDelete: Cascade)
  employee   Employee   @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)
  branch     Branch?    @relation(fields: [branchId], references: [branchId], onDelete: SetNull)

  @@index([attendanceId])
  @@index([empId])
  @@index([punchedAt])
  @@index([branchId])
  @@map("attendance_logs")
}

model LeaveType {
  leaveTypeId           Int                         @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("leave_type_id")
  code                  String                      @unique @db.VarChar(50)
  name                  String                      @db.VarChar(120)
  isPaid                Boolean                     @default(true) @map("is_paid")
  requiresAttachment    Boolean                     @default(false) @map("requires_attachment")
  status                RecordStatus                @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt             DateTime                    @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt             DateTime                    @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  leaves Leave[]

  @@map("leave_types")
}

model Leave {
  leaveId         Int         @id @default(autoincrement()) @map("leave_id")
  empId           Int         @map("emp_id")
  leaveTypeId     Int         @map("leave_type_id")
  dateFrom        DateTime    @map("date_from") @db.Date
  dateTo          DateTime    @map("date_to") @db.Date
  totalDays       Float       @map("total_days")
  reason          String      @db.Text
  attachment      String?     @db.VarChar(255)
  status          LeaveStatus @default(PENDING)
  approvedById    Int?        @map("approved_by")
  approvedAt      DateTime?   @map("approved_at")
  rejectionReason String?     @map("rejection_reason") @db.Text
  createdById     Int?        @map("created_by")
  createdAt       DateTime    @default(now()) @map("created_at")
  updatedAt       DateTime    @updatedAt @map("updated_at")

  employee   Employee  @relation(fields: [empId], references: [empId], onDelete: Cascade)
  leaveType  LeaveType @relation(fields: [leaveTypeId], references: [leaveTypeId], onDelete: Restrict)
  approvedBy User?     @relation("LeaveApprovedBy", fields: [approvedById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)
  createdBy  User?     @relation("LeaveCreatedBy", fields: [createdById], references: [userId], onDelete: SetNull)

  @@index([empId])
  @@index([leaveTypeId])
  @@index([status])
  @@index([approvedById])
  @@index([createdById])
  @@map("leaves")
}

FILE: src\lib\db\prisma.ts

import { PrismaMariaDb } from "@prisma/adapter-mariadb";
import { PrismaClient } from "../../generated/prisma/client";
import { env, isDevelopment } from "../env";

function getDatabaseName(databaseUrl: URL): string {
  const databaseName = databaseUrl.pathname.replace(/^\//, "");

  if (!databaseName) {
    throw new Error("DATABASE_URL must include a database name.");
  }

  return decodeURIComponent(databaseName);
}

function createPrismaAdapter() {
  const databaseUrl = new URL(env.DATABASE_URL);

  return new PrismaMariaDb({
    host: databaseUrl.hostname,
    port: databaseUrl.port ? Number(databaseUrl.port) : 3306,
    user: decodeURIComponent(databaseUrl.username),
    password: decodeURIComponent(databaseUrl.password),
    database: getDatabaseName(databaseUrl),
    connectionLimit: isDevelopment ? 5 : 10,
  });
}

const globalForPrisma = globalThis as unknown as {
  prisma?: PrismaClient;
};

export const prisma =
  globalForPrisma.prisma ??
  new PrismaClient({
    adapter: createPrismaAdapter(),
    log: isDevelopment ? ["warn", "error"] : ["error"],
  });

if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
  globalForPrisma.prisma = prisma;
}

"use server";

import {
  Prisma,
} from "@/generated/prisma/client";
import {
  revalidatePath,
} from "next/cache";
import {
  redirect,
} from "next/navigation";
import { requireCanManageEmployees } from "@/features/auth/server/permission-guards";
import { prisma } from "@/lib/db/prisma";
import {
  ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS,
  type AttendancePolicyActionState,
  type AttendancePolicyFormInput,
  type AttendancePolicyKey,
  type AttendancePolicyValueType,
} from "../types/attendance-policy-types";
import {
  ATTENDANCE_POLICY_DEFINITIONS,
} from "./attendance-policy-definitions";
import {
  getAttendancePolicyRuntimeConfig,
} from "./attendance-policy-queries";
import {
  parseAttendancePolicyFormData,
} from "../validators/attendance-policy-validation";

type ActiveBranchRow = {
  branchId:
    | number
    | bigint
    | string;
};

type PolicyWriteRow = {
  key:
    AttendancePolicyKey;

  value: string;

  valueType:
    AttendancePolicyValueType;

  description: string;
};

function definitionFor(
  key:
    AttendancePolicyKey,
) {
  const definition =
    ATTENDANCE_POLICY_DEFINITIONS.find(
      (candidate) =>
        candidate.key === key,
    );

  if (!definition) {
    throw new Error(
      `Attendance policy definition not found for ${key}.`,
    );
  }

  return definition;
}

function createWriteRow(
  key:
    AttendancePolicyKey,

  value: string,
): PolicyWriteRow {
  const definition =
    definitionFor(key);

  return {
    key,

    value,

    valueType:
      definition.valueType,

    description:
      definition.description,
  };
}

function buildWriteRows(
  input:
    AttendancePolicyFormInput,
): PolicyWriteRow[] {
  return [
    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.DEFAULT_BRANCH_ID,
      String(
        input.defaultBranchId,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.ALLOW_WEB_TIME_IN,
      String(
        input.allowWebTimeIn,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.ALLOW_MANUAL_TIME_IN,
      String(
        input.allowManualTimeIn,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.REQUIRE_PHOTO,
      String(
        input.requirePhoto,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.REQUIRE_LOCATION,
      String(
        input.requireLocation,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.PHOTO_DIRECTORY,
      input.photoDirectory,
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.MAX_PHOTO_SIZE_MB,
      String(
        input.maxPhotoSizeMb,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.LATE_GRACE_MINUTES,
      String(
        input.lateGraceMinutes,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.AUTO_MARK_MISSING_TIMEOUT,
      String(
        input.autoMarkMissingTimeout,
      ),
    ),

    createWriteRow(
      ATTENDANCE_POLICY_KEYS.MISSING_TIMEOUT_MINUTES,
      String(
        input.missingTimeoutMinutes,
      ),
    ),
  ];
}

async function activeBranchExists(
  branchId: number,
): Promise<boolean> {
  const rows =
    await prisma.$queryRaw<
      ActiveBranchRow[]
    >`
      SELECT
        branch_id AS branchId
      FROM branches
      WHERE
        branch_id = ${branchId}
        AND status = 'ACTIVE'
      LIMIT 1
    `;

  return rows.length > 0;
}

function revalidateAttendancePolicyPaths(): void {
  revalidatePath(
    "/dashboard/settings",
  );

  revalidatePath(
    "/dashboard/settings/attendance-policies",
  );

  revalidatePath(
    "/dashboard/attendance",
  );

  revalidatePath(
    "/dashboard/attendance/manual",
  );

  revalidatePath(
    "/dashboard/attendance/automation",
  );
}

export async function updateAttendancePolicyAction(
  _previousState:
    AttendancePolicyActionState,

  formData: FormData,
): Promise<AttendancePolicyActionState> {
  await requireCanManageEmployees();

  const parsed =
    parseAttendancePolicyFormData(
      formData,
    );

  if (!parsed.ok) {
    return {
      status: "ERROR",

      message:
        "Review the highlighted Attendance Policy fields and try again.",

      fieldErrors:
        parsed.fieldErrors,
    };
  }

  const branchExists =
    await activeBranchExists(
      parsed.data.defaultBranchId,
    );

  if (!branchExists) {
    return {
      status: "ERROR",

      message:
        "The selected default branch is unavailable.",

      fieldErrors: {
        defaultBranchId: [
          "Select an active branch.",
        ],
      },
    };
  }

  const oldResolved =
    await getAttendancePolicyRuntimeConfig();

  const writeRows =
    buildWriteRows(
      parsed.data,
    );

  try {
    await prisma.$transaction(
      async (
        tx:
          Prisma.TransactionClient,
      ) => {
        for (const row of writeRows) {
          await tx.$executeRaw`
            INSERT INTO attendance_policy_settings (
              setting_key,
              setting_value,
              value_type,
              description,
              created_at,
              updated_at
            )
            VALUES (
              ${row.key},
              ${row.value},
              ${row.valueType},
              ${row.description},
              NOW(3),
              NOW(3)
            )
            ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
              setting_value =
                VALUES(setting_value),
              value_type =
                VALUES(value_type),
              description =
                VALUES(description),
              updated_at =
                NOW(3)
          `;
        }

        await tx.activityLog.create({
          data: {
            actorUserId: null,

            action:
              "ATTENDANCE_POLICY_UPDATED_V1",

            entityType:
              "attendance_policy",

            entityId:
              "GLOBAL",

            oldValue: {
              config:
                oldResolved.config,

              sourceMap:
                oldResolved.sourceMap,
            },

            newValue: {
              config:
                parsed.data,

              source:
                "DATABASE",

              changedKeys:
                writeRows.map(
                  (row) =>
                    row.key,
                ),

              permissionGuard:
                "requireCanManageEmployees",
            },
          },
        });
      },
    );
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(
      "Unable to update Attendance Policies:",
      error,
    );

    return {
      status: "ERROR",

      message:
        "The Attendance Policies could not be saved.",

      fieldErrors: {},
    };
  }

  revalidateAttendancePolicyPaths();

  redirect(
    "/dashboard/settings/attendance-policies?notice=updated",
  );
}

FILE: src\features\settings\attendance-policies\validators\attendance-policy-validation.ts

import { z } from "zod";
import type {
  AttendancePolicyActionState,
  AttendancePolicyFormField,
  AttendancePolicyFormInput,
} from "../types/attendance-policy-types";

const relativeDirectorySchema =
  z
    .string()
    .trim()
    .min(
      1,
      "Photo directory is required.",
    )
    .max(
      191,
      "Photo directory cannot exceed 191 characters.",
    )
    .regex(
      /^[A-Za-z0-9/_-]+$/,
      "Use letters, numbers, forward slashes, underscores, and hyphens only.",
    )
    .refine(
      (value) =>
        !value.includes(".."),
      "Parent-directory traversal is not allowed.",
    )
    .refine(
      (value) =>
        !value.startsWith("/"),
      "Use a relative directory, not an absolute path.",
    )
    .transform((value) =>
      value.replace(/\/+$/u, ""),
    );

export const attendancePolicyFormSchema =
  z.object({
    defaultBranchId:
      z.coerce
        .number()
        .int()
        .positive(
          "Select an active default branch.",
        ),

    allowWebTimeIn:
      z.boolean(),

    allowManualTimeIn:
      z.boolean(),

    requirePhoto:
      z.boolean(),

    requireLocation:
      z.boolean(),

    photoDirectory:
      relativeDirectorySchema,

    maxPhotoSizeMb:
      z.coerce
        .number()
        .int()
        .min(
          1,
          "Maximum photo size must be at least 1 MB.",
        )
        .max(
          25,
          "Maximum photo size cannot exceed 25 MB.",
        ),

    lateGraceMinutes:
      z.coerce
        .number()
        .int()
        .min(
          0,
          "Late grace cannot be negative.",
        )
        .max(
          180,
          "Late grace cannot exceed 180 minutes.",
        ),

    autoMarkMissingTimeout:
      z.boolean(),

    missingTimeoutMinutes:
      z.coerce
        .number()
        .int()
        .min(
          60,
          "Missing time-out threshold must be at least 60 minutes.",
        )
        .max(
          2880,
          "Missing time-out threshold cannot exceed 2,880 minutes.",
        ),
  });

export type AttendancePolicyFormParseResult =
  | {
      ok: true;

      data:
        AttendancePolicyFormInput;
    }
  | {
      ok: false;

      fieldErrors: Partial<
        Record<
          AttendancePolicyFormField,
          string[]
        >
      >;
    };

function readString(
  formData: FormData,
  name: string,
): string {
  const value =
    formData.get(name);

  return typeof value === "string"
    ? value
    : "";
}

function readCheckbox(
  formData: FormData,
  name: string,
): boolean {
  const value =
    formData.get(name);

  return (
    value === "on" ||
    value === "true" ||
    value === "1"
  );
}

export function parseAttendancePolicyFormData(
  formData: FormData,
): AttendancePolicyFormParseResult {
  const result =
    attendancePolicyFormSchema.safeParse({
      defaultBranchId:
        readString(
          formData,
          "defaultBranchId",
        ),

      allowWebTimeIn:
        readCheckbox(
          formData,
          "allowWebTimeIn",
        ),

      allowManualTimeIn:
        readCheckbox(
          formData,
          "allowManualTimeIn",
        ),

      requirePhoto:
        readCheckbox(
          formData,
          "requirePhoto",
        ),

      requireLocation:
        readCheckbox(
          formData,
          "requireLocation",
        ),

      photoDirectory:
        readString(
          formData,
          "photoDirectory",
        ),

      maxPhotoSizeMb:
        readString(
          formData,
          "maxPhotoSizeMb",
        ),

      lateGraceMinutes:
        readString(
          formData,
          "lateGraceMinutes",
        ),

      autoMarkMissingTimeout:
        readCheckbox(
          formData,
          "autoMarkMissingTimeout",
        ),

      missingTimeoutMinutes:
        readString(
          formData,
          "missingTimeoutMinutes",
        ),
    });

  if (result.success) {
    return {
      ok: true,
      data: result.data,
    };
  }

  const fieldErrors: Partial<
    Record<
      AttendancePolicyFormField,
      string[]
    >
  > = {};

  for (const issue of result.error.issues) {
    const field =
      issue.path[0];

    if (typeof field !== "string") {
      continue;
    }

    const typedField =
      field as AttendancePolicyFormField;

    fieldErrors[typedField] = [
      ...(fieldErrors[typedField] ?? []),
      issue.message,
    ];
  }

  return {
    ok: false,
    fieldErrors,
  };
}

export const INITIAL_ATTENDANCE_POLICY_ACTION_STATE: AttendancePolicyActionState =
  {
    status: "IDLE",

    message: "",

    fieldErrors: {},
  };

============================================================
FILE: src\features\auth\server\permission-guards.ts
============================================================

import "server-only";

import { notFound, redirect } from "next/navigation";
import {
  canManageEmployees,
  canManageLeaves,
  canManageRfid,
  canManageSettings,
  canViewAllAttendance,
  canViewAuditLogs,
} from "@/lib/security/roles";
import { getCurrentSession } from "./session";

export async function requireAuthenticatedUser() {
  const session = await getCurrentSession();

  if (!session) {
    redirect("/login");
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanManageEmployees() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canManageEmployees(session.role)) {
    notFound();
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanManageRfid() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canManageRfid(session.role)) {
    notFound();
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanManageLeaves() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canManageLeaves(session.role)) {
    notFound();
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanViewAuditLogs() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canViewAuditLogs(session.role)) {
    notFound();
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanManageSettings() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canManageSettings(session.role)) {
    notFound();
  }

  return session;
}

export async function requireCanViewAllAttendance() {
  const session = await requireAuthenticatedUser();

  if (!canViewAllAttendance(session.role)) {
    redirect("/dashboard/attendance/odl");
  }

  return session;
}
